Or input your stakekey, address or $adahandle below and look at your own statistics

# Twitter Raids - Palantir

![](/blurred/tmoblack-400x400.png)

Twitter Raids
-------------

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Last queried Mallard Order Siege Bot: | one year ago |

*   Active Raids
*   Past Raids 1401

Active Raids
------------

Head over to [_The Crypt_](https://discord.com/invite/mallardorder)
 and check the #twitter-raid channel for raids to join!

Don't forget to verify/link your twitter account in #twitter-verify so you are eligible to earn $RUNE rewards and can start climbing the [leaderboard](/topraiders)
!

Santa's Workshop

# About - Palantir

![](/blurred/0555-480x480.png)

About
-----

![](/0555-480x480.png)

"Don't Trust, Verify."
----------------------

This website is just a hobby project by me (tehsoul) and is not to be considered an official Mallard Order project in any way, shape or form.  
I am a software architect by profession and am used to dabbling in code, frontend (especially websites) not so much...  
Should you be a fellow mallard with superior web dev skills to make this site really shine and want to take on the frontend part - let me know!

All data used to build this project is publicly available on the Cardano blockchain.

Please be aware that I am inevitably bound to break things every so often  
(I do have the intention of adding some extra features over time and will publish new versions as I go along).

Don't hesitate to hit me up on discord if you have any questions or (reasonable) suggestions.

![](/sparechange.gif)

Should you **really** like what you see, please consider donating some ADA to $tehsoul  
Any donations will go towards my Blockfrost subscription and website hosting to keep the seeing stone powered up.

### Market - Ceiling

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Marketplace data as of: | 9 months ago |

For mallard shopping, fellow community member [Sirez](https://twitter.com/SirezADA)
 made a **fantastic** [chrome extension](https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/jpgstore-extension-by-cnf/emndkdeeljnhblojmnbdfhjjeoikdcek?hl=en&authuser=0)
 that overlays the RUNE staking rewards on Mallards while you're browsing JPG Store!

 Toggle RUNE staking rewards

 Toggle rarest traits

![](https://images.cnft.tools/ipfs/Qmc9S5gnjNPTas7oaawf7kgyUz7zZGgzp8oYLwpgAKBSr4)

Note that the values in below are _points_ and not _counts_ of likes, retweets and replies.  
The points given for each interaction can theoretically differ from raid to raid, but are usually as follows:  
Like: 1 point, Retweet: 2 points, Reply: 5 points.

  **PROTIP!** if you Login with your user will be highlighted in the leaderboard!
